msg:It has been two days since I left the store. I have stayed in hotels all over the years so many times. To be honest, I seldom write down my feelings.
However, although the Beijing itinerary this time was only two days, the contrast between before and after really made me feel deeply. The beautiful woman in Liaoning Mansion (like Lu Yao on the nameplate), with her capable and thoughtful service, warm and thorough communication, gave me a very good ending to my trip between Xi'an and Beijing.

I really can't help but want to say two more words:
It is really not easy to be a full-time researcher. The reporting task was suddenly and frequently moved to different cities. This time, it was less than a day from Xi'an to fly to Beijing.
Let me talk about Xi'an first. Although I am a Gold Diamond member of Ctrip, when I checked the meeting place, I was tempted by the low price of the AutoNavi link**, so I decided on the Sheraton in Chanba, Xi'an (meeting place) by accident. But later the conference affairs group notified that the conference affairs group will bear the accommodation and registration fees of the experts. Then, I will communicate with the hotel, **.
The ridiculous thing is that **replied and communicated to no avail, the hotel disagreed and let me check in normally. There were too many things that day, my fire was ignited immediately, and after a reasonable coordination and communication, it was cancelled. However, there is a shadow: firstly, ** will never touch again, and secondly, the platform and the hotel are not willing to take the initiative to be responsible for the guests. the foothold.
In less than 24 hours, land in Beijing. With the excitement of **, I returned to Ctrip in a down-to-earth manner. Although I had always planned to live in Liaoning Mansion, there were only high-priced houses left in Liaoning Mansion on the night of landing, so I chose Weishi in Beihang University. These two came to Beijing before, and actually lived there many times. However, I didn't expect the difference to be so big now.

The quality of all aspects of reception at the front desk of Reality is very insufficient, not because of a bad attitude, but because of a lack of quality. I also work in a university, and I know the operation mode of the international exchange center of a university. At first I thought it was a part-time job for Beihang students, so I understood. But when I checked out the next day, I found that it should not be a part-time job for undergraduates. I won't comment too much on the specific details, after all, I have a good relationship with colleagues in Beihang University.

The next morning in Beijing, I rushed to Liaoning Building with a heart that was tossed at a loss by the platform and the hotel. Here, I have lived in Beijing many times before. The overall feeling is okay, but not exclusive. This time, in addition to myself, there were two other colleagues who negotiated and reported to the Chinese Academy of Sciences. I ordered 3 rooms on Ctrip. I will check in first and wait for them. But when I arrived, it was just after 8 o'clock in the morning. Moreover, the third senior said that the itinerary has changed, but he will not come. I can only come to the front desk with the attitude of giving it a try (after all, I have just been tossed about, after all, I know the average level of hotel service in Beijing).

Very lucky, this lady at the front desk turned the aura around me completely üëçüëçüåπ. I won't go into details one by one. I think the most important thing is that she has the purpose of "convenient travel for guests" that I mentioned before. After a clear understanding of the situation and my needs, I communicated skillfully with colleagues in the reservation depar**ent and Ctrip, and made arrangements for "unsubscription, room upgrade, floor assignment, and check-in process for other guests" smoothly and quickly. The whole process seemed to be smooth. to 5 minutes.

To be honest, I saw light in her heart and eyes.
As a passenger, what you need most of the time is smoothness and convenience, not how much you pay when you are haggling. However, I think the most uncomfortable thing is being restricted by the hotel and the platform to "must stay late for check-in". These should be the foundation for platforms and hotels as service providers to do better.

On the second day after staying in Liaoning Hotel, the report and communication were smooth, and we decided to leave the hotel and return to Shenyang in advance. When I checked out, I wanted to say thank you to her face to face. Unfortunately, she should not be on duty. Hope to see her again next time. I will definitely come to Liaoning Mansion again. However, I think that everyone knows and feels that whether tourists are willing to live there depends on more factors than facilities, price, or even the respectful service that reveals the flavor of profit. It is the thoughtfulness, trust, and care that are for the sake of passengers, and the light in her heart and eyes.

When I got up in the morning, I saw the demand for this evaluation pushed by Ctrip, and I felt it. I didn‚Äôt expect that I would write so much on a public platformüòÄ. Perhaps, subconsciously, I don't want our society to become too procedural, materialized, and superficially profit-oriented. I sincerely hope that no matter whether it is a platform or a hotel, they can carefully manage the humanistic meaning and far-reaching value of this beam of light in the eyes of Ms. Lu Yao.

Thank you, I will stay here again next time, I hope to meet many Miss Luüëç.
